The field pays even money if the next roll is a 3, 4, 9, 10 or 11; 2 to 1 if a 2 is rolled, and 3 to 1 on twelve (some tables only pay 2:1).
You lose if the next roll is a 5, 6, 7 or 8. This popular bet gives the house a relatively small 2.77% edge (5.55% if "12" only pays double).
However, we still don't recommend this bet, as much better odds can be found on the Craps table.
The "Big" means big advantage for the house, and big mistake for the player. Since the house only pays even money, it has a 9.09% advantage.
If you want to wager on this number, consider making a "place" bet instead - it will pay 7 to 6 (with correct units bet) instead of even money, trimming the casino's percentage to a meagre 1.52%.
The house edge on this point is 6.67%
This bet gives the casino a 4.00% advantage.
The house only has a 1.515% edge on this bet, which makes it comparable to the 1.414% and 1.402% edges on the pass and don't-pass lines.
However, we do not recommend this bet, because you cannot take advantage of free odds, as you could by making pass, don't-pass, come and don't-come bets.
This one-roll bet only wins if a 2, 3 or 12 is rolled. The chances of rolling craps are 1 in 9; the house only pays 7 to 1, which means the house has an 11.11% edge.
This bet wins if the next roll totals 11, and loses on any other roll.
Like all proposition bets, the odds are stacked significantly against you. On the "Eleven" bet, the house holds a 16.67% advantage over the player.
This is a combination "any craps" and "eleven" bet, which means that it wins if the next roll is a 2, 3, 11 or 12; all other totals lose.
It pays 3 to 1 on "craps", 7 to 1 on "eleven"
There are 4 ways to win 3 units and 2 ways to win 7 units out of 36 rolls; this gives the house an 11.11% edge on this bet.
This bet only pays if the next roll is a %d all other totals lose this bet.
The true odds of making this point are 36 to 1, the casino only pays 29 to 1 (30 FOR 1); this sucker bet gives the house a 16.67%% edge.
This bet only pays if the next roll totals three (1-2 or 2-1 on the dice), all other totals lose.
Since there are 2 ways out of 36 to roll a three; the true odds are 18 to 1. The 15 FOR 1 (14 to 1) paid by the casino gives them a 16.67% edge.
(It's just like donating the money to the casino, except you can't deduct it from your taxes!)
If the next roll is a seven; this bet wins.
Any other total loses.
Seven is the most likely number to be rolled, at 6 ways out of 36 (1 out of 6 chance). However, the casino only pays 4 to 1 on this bet, giving the house a 16.67% edge. Save your money for the show.

@Recommend
Casinos take a very high margin on Keno, typically 29%.
Although you can potentially win a million dollars from a bet of just a few dollars the chances of this happening are remote.
The best chance of winning is to play those games which have smaller jackpots, but better payoffs for the more likely number of hits that you will score, eg All Catches.

Keno Coach - Forty Forty Tickets
This game is a variation on the normal forty number game.  Instead of picking a set of forty numbers it compares the spread of numbers picked, either top and bottom or left and right.
No numbers are highlighted in these games as you are comparing one side to the other.  Each side has it's own colour for drawn numbers.
Keno Coach - Forty Forty Tickets
This game is a variation on the normal forty number game.  Instead of picking a set of forty numbers it compares the spread of numbers picked, either top and bottom or left and right.
No numbers are highlighted in these games as you are comparing one side to the other.  Each side has it's own colour for drawn numbers.

Keno Coach - Bet Against
Pick between 8 and 15 numbers.
You only win if none of the numbers you picked are drawn by the Keno machine.
Keno Coach - Catch All
 Pick between 2 and 7 numbers.
You only win if the Keno machine draws all the numbers you picked.
Keno Coach - Last Ball Drawn
Pick between 1 and 6 numbers.
If the last number drawn by the Keno machine is one you picked and all your other numbers have been drawn, then your winnings will be doubled subject to a casino maximum of $100,000,000

The payout odds on this machine are higher than the standard ticket game.
